 What is it? Parole law experts say that there are two types of parole, first custody parole and second regular parole
 castady parole us sthiti main di jaati he, jab kaidi ke parivaar main kisi kii maut jaae yaa phir parivaar main kisi kii shaadi ho yaa phir parivaar main koi bahut biimaar ho
 In addition, custodial parole is given in very special circumstances
 castady parole ke liye kaidi jail adheekshak ko aavedan karata he
 If the jail administration rejects the application, then an appeal can be made in the court
 castady parole ke dauraan aaropee yaa doshi ko police abhiraksha main jail se baahar laayaa jaataa he
 Its maximum duration is 6 hours
 regular parole doshi kaidi ko hi di jaati he
 It is not provided for under trial prisoner
 isamen doshi ke liye ek samay seemaa bhi nirdhaarit hoti he
 Regular parole is not awarded to convicted offenders who have committed murder after the rape and have been convicted
 parole paane ke liye kaidi kaa bhartiya naagarik hona bhi zaruri he
 Those convicted of terrorism or treason cases cannot be granted parole
 regular parole ek baar main ek maah ke liye di jaati he
 In special case it can be increased
 kanoonee jaankaron ke mutabik parole kaa faisla prashasnic hota he
 If the parole application from the jail administration and the home department is rejected, then the guilty can go to court
 parole kaa aavedan vahi kaidi kar saktaa he, jo sajaa kaat rahaa ho
 No application of this should be under consideration in any court
 parole kuch vishesh paristhitiyon main hi di jaati he
 The condition is that the prisoner's conduct should be good in prison
